Context:
ORACLE SOA DEHYDRATION Oracle SOA dehydration is the process of persisting the state of long-running BPEL processes into the dehydration store database. Why dehydration exists: - Long-running processes should not stay in JVM memory indefinitely. - Oracle persists process state to the database. - When needed, the process is rehydrated and resumed. Common dehydration triggers: - wait activity - receive activity - callback invocation - asynchronous partner links - human workflow pauses Dehydration store: - stored in Oracle database - tables hold instance state - engine reloads state when required Common issues: - stuck instances - dehydration store growth - slow DB performance - stale call
Source: oracle\dehydration.txt
User: Give a practical answer based on this ORACLE context.

================================================================================ TOKENIZATION STRATEGIES IN NLP ================================================================================ 1. WHAT IS TOKENIZATION? ------------------------ The process of breaking down a raw string of text into smaller units called "tokens." These tokens are then mapped to numerical IDs that the model can understand. 2. MAJOR METHODS ---------------- * Word-level: Splits by whitespace. Problem: Huge vocabulary and "Out of Vocabulary" (OOV) issues. * Character-level: Splits into individual letters. Problem: Very long sequences and loss of semantic meaning. * Subword-level: The modern standard. Bre

================================================================================ ATTENTION MECHANISMS: SCALED DOT-PRODUCT & MULTI-HEAD ================================================================================ 1. CORE CONCEPT --------------- Attention allows the model to focus on specific parts of the input sequence when producing a specific part of the output. It calculates a "relevance score" between tokens. 2. SCALED DOT-PRODUCT ATTENTION ------------------------------- The mechanism uses three primary vectors: * Query (Q): What I am looking for. * Key (K): What I have to offer. * Value (V): The information I provide. Formula: Attention(Q, K, V) = softmax((QK^T) / sqrt(d_k))V
Source: ai\attention.txt

Context:
ORACLE SOA DEHYDRATION Oracle SOA dehydration is the process of persisting the state of long-running BPEL processes into the dehydration store database. Why dehydration exists: - Long-running processes should not stay in JVM memory indefinitely. - Oracle persists process state to the database. - When needed, the process is rehydrated and resumed. Common dehydration triggers: - wait activity - receive activity - callback invocation - asynchronous partner links - human workflow pauses Dehydration store: - stored in Oracle database - tables hold instance state - engine reloads state when required Common issues: - stuck instances - dehydration store growth - slow DB performance - stale call
Source: oracle\dehydration.txt

================================================================================ ATTENTION MECHANISMS: SCALED DOT-PRODUCT & MULTI-HEAD ================================================================================ 1. CORE CONCEPT --------------- Attention allows the model to focus on specific parts of the input sequence when producing a specific part of the output. It calculates a "relevance score" between tokens. 2. SCALED DOT-PRODUCT ATTENTION ------------------------------- The mechanism uses three primary vectors: * Query (Q): What I am looking for. * Key (K): What I have to offer. * Value (V): The information I provide. Formula: Attention(Q, K, V) = softmax((QK^T) / sqrt(d_k))V

Context:
ORACLE SOA DEHYDRATION Oracle SOA dehydration is the process of persisting the state of long-running BPEL processes into the dehydration store database. Why dehydration exists: - Long-running processes should not stay in JVM memory indefinitely. - Oracle persists process state to the database. - When needed, the process is rehydrated and resumed. Common dehydration triggers: - wait activity - receive activity - callback invocation - asynchronous partner links - human workflow pauses Dehydration store: - stored in Oracle database - tables hold instance state - engine reloads state when required Common issues: - stuck instances - dehydration store growth - slow DB performance - stale call
Source: oracle\dehydration.txt

================================================================================ ATTENTION MECHANISMS: SCALED DOT-PRODUCT & MULTI-HEAD ================================================================================ 1. CORE CONCEPT --------------- Attention allows the model to focus on specific parts of the input sequence when producing a specific part of the output. It calculates a "relevance score" between tokens. 2. SCALED DOT-PRODUCT ATTENTION ------------------------------- The mechanism uses three primary vectors: * Query (Q): What I am looking for. * Key (K): What I have to offer. * Value (V): The information I provide. Formula: Attention(Q, K, V) = softmax((QK^T) / sqrt(d_k))V
Source: ai\attention.txt
